if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: ajax.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('ajax.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): ajax.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('ajax.php') != '8adc3ab61806e2fbde6e6930d83d8c4f96d4a0e2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('ajax.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of ajax.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '8adc3ab61806e2fbde6e6930d83d8c4f96d4a0e2') {
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '6e8a0d07058d123e2655b5319a8a8f23d63bf369') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: ajax.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('ajax.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('ajax.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('ajax.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('ajax.php') !== '8adc3ab61806e2fbde6e6930d83d8c4f96d4a0e2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): ajax.php');
		}
	}
}

	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') != '898044fa339f5b9969711dee668432a79ee125a7') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '898044fa339f5b9969711dee668432a79ee125a7') {

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php') !== '898044fa339f5b9969711dee668432a79ee125a7') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/classes/OIDplus.class.php');

	writefile_6();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php') != '2a80b4e1467ff72e824cb77a1ac263479f10912c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php') !== '2a80b4e1467ff72e824cb77a1ac263479f10912c') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php') !== 'e6a85a455026a615229ff89439020249b2f38129') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php');

			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_6();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php') !== '2a80b4e1467ff72e824cb77a1ac263479f10912c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/db_updates/update204.inc.php');

	}
